FILE: frontend\src\app\login\page.tsx
============================================================
'use client';

import { useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
import { z } from 'zod';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Form, FormControl, FormField, FormItem, FormLabel, FormMessage } from '@/components/ui/form';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { authAPI } from '@/lib/authAPI';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

const formSchema = z.object({
  email: z.string().email({
    message: 'Please enter a valid email address.',
  }),
  password: z.string().min(1, {
    message: 'Password is required.',
  }),
});

export default function LoginPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

  const form = useForm<z.infer<typeof formSchema>>({
    resolver: zodResolver(formSchema),
    defaultValues: {
      email: '',
      password: '',
    },
  });

  async function onSubmit(values: z.infer<typeof formSchema>) {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const response = await authAPI.login(values.email, values.password);

      // Save the token and user ID to localStorage
      localStorage.setItem('access_token', response.access_token);
      localStorage.setItem('user_id', response.user_id);

      toast.success('Logged in successfully!');
      router.push('/dashboard');
      router.refresh();
    } catch (error: any) {
      console.error('Login error:', error);
      toast.error(error.response?.data?.detail || 'Login failed');
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gradient-to-br from-teal-50 to-cyan-100 dark:from-teal-900/20 dark:to-cyan-900/20 p-4">
      <Card className="w-full max-w-md shadow-lg dark:bg-gray-800 dark:border-gray-700">
        <CardHeader className="space-y-1">
          <CardTitle className="text-2xl font-bold text-center text-teal-800 dark:text-teal-200">Welcome Back</CardTitle>
          <CardDescription className="text-center text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400">
            Sign in to your account to continue
          </CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <Form {...form}>
            <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="space-y-4">
              <FormField
                control={form.control}
                name="email"
                render={({ field }) => (
                  <FormItem>
                    <FormLabel className="dark:text-gray-200">Email</FormLabel>
                    <FormControl>
                      <Input placeholder="john@example.com" type="email" {...field} className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 dark:text-white" />
                    </FormControl>
                    <FormMessage />
                  </FormItem>
                )}
              />
              <FormField
                control={form.control}
                name="password"
                render={({ field }) => (
                  <FormItem>
                    <FormLabel className="dark:text-gray-200">Password</FormLabel>
                    <FormControl>
                      <Input type="password" placeholder="‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢" {...field} className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 dark:text-white" />
                    </FormControl>
                    <FormMessage />
                  </FormItem>
                )}
              />
              <Button type="submit" className="w-full bg-teal-600 hover:bg-teal-700 dark:bg-teal-700 dark:hover:bg-teal-800" disabled={isLoading}>
                {isLoading ? 'Signing in...' : 'Sign In'}
              </Button>
            </form>
          </Form>
          <div className="mt-4 text-center text-sm text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400">
            Don't have an account?{' '}
            <a href="/signup" className="font-medium text-teal-600 hover:text-teal-500 dark:text-teal-400 dark:hover:text-teal-300">
              Sign up
            </a>
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: frontend\src\app\signup\page.tsx
============================================================
'use client';

import { useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/navigation';
import { zodResolver } from '@hookform/resolvers/zod';
import { useForm } from 'react-hook-form';
import { z } from 'zod';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Form, FormControl, FormField, FormItem, FormLabel, FormMessage } from '@/components/ui/form';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Card, CardContent, CardDescription, CardHeader, CardTitle } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { authAPI } from '@/lib/authAPI';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

const formSchema = z.object({
  username: z.string().min(2, {
    message: 'Username must be at least 2 characters.',
  }),
  email: z.string().email({
    message: 'Please enter a valid email address.',
  }),
  password: z.string().min(6, {
    message: 'Password must be at least 6 characters.',
  }),
});

export default function SignupPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

  const form = useForm<z.infer<typeof formSchema>>({
    resolver: zodResolver(formSchema),
    defaultValues: {
      username: '',
      email: '',
      password: '',
    },
  });

  async function onSubmit(values: z.infer<typeof formSchema>) {
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const response = await authAPI.signup(values);

      toast.success('Account created successfully!');
      router.push('/login');
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Signup error:', error);
      toast.error('Failed to create account. Please try again.');
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-gradient-to-br from-teal-50 to-cyan-100 dark:from-teal-900/20 dark:to-cyan-900/20 p-4">
      <Card className="w-full max-w-md shadow-lg dark:bg-gray-800 dark:border-gray-700">
        <CardHeader className="space-y-1">
          <CardTitle className="text-2xl font-bold text-center text-teal-800 dark:text-teal-200">Create Account</CardTitle>
          <CardDescription className="text-center text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400">
            Enter your details to create a new account
          </CardDescription>
        </CardHeader>
        <CardContent>
          <Form {...form}>
            <form onSubmit={form.handleSubmit(onSubmit)} className="space-y-4">
              <FormField
                control={form.control}
                name="username"
                render={({ field }) => (
                  <FormItem>
                    <FormLabel className="dark:text-gray-200">Username</FormLabel>
                    <FormControl>
                      <Input placeholder="johndoe" {...field} className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 dark:text-white" />
                    </FormControl>
                    <FormMessage />
                  </FormItem>
                )}
              />
              <FormField
                control={form.control}
                name="email"
                render={({ field }) => (
                  <FormItem>
                    <FormLabel className="dark:text-gray-200">Email</FormLabel>
                    <FormControl>
                      <Input placeholder="john@example.com" type="email" {...field} className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 dark:text-white" />
                    </FormControl>
                    <FormMessage />
                  </FormItem>
                )}
              />
              <FormField
                control={form.control}
                name="password"
                render={({ field }) => (
                  <FormItem>
                    <FormLabel className="dark:text-gray-200">Password</FormLabel>
                    <FormControl>
                      <Input type="password" placeholder="‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢" {...field} className="bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 dark:text-white" />
                    </FormControl>
                    <FormMessage />
                  </FormItem>
                )}
              />
              <Button type="submit" className="w-full bg-teal-600 hover:bg-teal-700 dark:bg-teal-700 dark:hover:bg-teal-800" disabled={isLoading}>
                {isLoading ? 'Creating Account...' : 'Sign Up'}
              </Button>
            </form>
          </Form>
          <div className="mt-4 text-center text-sm text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400">
            Already have an account?{' '}
            <a href="/login" className="font-medium text-teal-600 hover:text-teal-500 dark:text-teal-400 dark:hover:text-teal-300">
              Sign in
            </a>
          </div>
        </CardContent>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: frontend\src\components\ChatButton.tsx
============================================================
'use client';

import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Bot } from 'lucide-react';
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import dynamic from 'next/dynamic';

// Dynamically import ChatInterface to avoid SSR issues
const ChatInterface = dynamic(() => import('./ChatInterface'), { ssr: false });

interface ChatButtonProps {
  userId?: string;
  onTaskUpdate?: () => void;
}

export default function ChatButton({ userId: propUserId, onTaskUpdate }: ChatButtonProps) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [effectiveUserId, setEffectiveUserId] = useState('');

  useEffect(() => {
    // Use the userId from props if provided, otherwise try to get from localStorage
    const userId = propUserId || localStorage.getItem('user_id') || localStorage.getItem('current_user_id') || localStorage.getItem('user_id') || '';
    setEffectiveUserId(userId);
  }, [propUserId]);

  const toggleChat = () => {
    setIsOpen(!isOpen);
  };

  return (
    <>
      <Button
        onClick={toggleChat}
        className="fixed bottom-6 right-6 z-50 w-14 h-14 rounded-full shadow-lg bg-teal-600 hover:bg-teal-700 dark:bg-teal-700 dark:hover:bg-teal-800"
        aria-label="Open AI Assistant"
      >
        <Bot className="h-6 w-6" />
      </Button>

      {isOpen && (
        <div className="fixed bottom-20 right-6 z-50 w-80 h-96 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800 rounded-lg shadow-xl border border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 overflow-hidden">
          <ChatInterface userId={effectiveUserId} onClose={() => setIsOpen(false)} onTaskUpdate={onTaskUpdate} />
        </div>
      )}
    </>
  );
}

============================================================
FILE: frontend\src\components\ChatInterface.tsx
============================================================
'use client';

import { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Send, X } from 'lucide-react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';

interface Message {
  id: string;
  content: string;
  role: 'user' | 'assistant';
  timestamp: Date;
}

interface ChatInterfaceProps {
  userId: string;
  onClose: () => void;
  onTaskUpdate?: () => void; // Function to refresh task list
}

export default function ChatInterface({ userId: propUserId, onClose, onTaskUpdate }: ChatInterfaceProps) {
  const [inputMessage, setInputMessage] = useState('');
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([
    {
      id: '1',
      content: 'How can I help with your tasks?',
      role: 'assistant',
      timestamp: new Date(),
    }
  ]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [effectiveUserId, setEffectiveUserId] = useState('');
  const scrollAreaRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  // Sync the user ID from props or localStorage
  useEffect(() => {
    const userId = propUserId || localStorage.getItem('user_id') || localStorage.getItem('current_user_id') || '';
    setEffectiveUserId(userId);

    // Log error if userId is missing but don't show it to user
    if (!userId) {
      console.error('User ID not found, using empty string');
    }
  }, [propUserId]);

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!inputMessage.trim() || isLoading) return;

    // Add user message to chat
    const userMessage: Message = {
      id: Date.now().toString(),
      content: inputMessage,
      role: 'user',
      timestamp: new Date(),
    };

    setMessages(prev => [...prev, userMessage]);
    setInputMessage('');
    setIsLoading(true);

    try {
      // Ensure we have a valid user ID before making the request
      if (!effectiveUserId) {
        throw new Error('User not authenticated');
      }

      // Call the backend chat API
      const response = await fetch(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL || 'http://127.0.0.1:8000'}/api/${effectiveUserId}/chat`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          'Authorization': `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('access_token') || ''}`
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          message: inputMessage,
          conversation_id: null // Will use/create a conversation
        }),
      });

      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
      }

      const data = await response.json();

      // Add assistant response to chat
      const assistantMessage: Message = {
        id: (Date.now() + 1).toString(),
        content: data.response,
        role: 'assistant',
        timestamp: new Date(),
      };

      setMessages(prev => [...prev, assistantMessage]);

      // Trigger real-time task sync if the agent performed actions
      if (data.actions && data.actions.length > 0) {
        // Call the refresh function if provided
        if (onTaskUpdate) {
          onTaskUpdate();
        }

        // Dispatch a custom event to notify other components about the changes
        window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('tasksUpdated', { detail: { actions: data.actions } }));

        // Specifically handle create_task success to refresh the task list
        const createActions = data.actions.filter((action: any) => action.action === 'create_task');
        if (createActions.length > 0) {
          // Dispatch a specific event for task creation
          window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('taskCreated', { detail: { actions: createActions } }));
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error sending message:', error);
      let errorMessageContent = 'Sorry, I encountered an error. Please try again.';

      // Check if it's a fetch error with response details
      if (error instanceof Error) {
        if (error.message.includes('fetch')) {
          errorMessageContent = 'Network error: Unable to connect to the server. Please check your connection.';
        } else if (error.message.includes('401')) {
          errorMessageContent = 'Authentication error: Please log in again.';
        } else if (error.message.includes('404')) {
          errorMessageContent = 'Resource not found: The requested resource could not be found.';
        } else {
          errorMessageContent = `Error: ${error.message}`;
        }
      }

      const errorMessage: Message = {
        id: (Date.now() + 1).toString(),
        content: errorMessageContent,
        role: 'assistant',
        timestamp: new Date(),
      };
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, errorMessage]);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // Auto-scroll to bottom when messages change
  useEffect(() => {
    if (scrollAreaRef.current) {
      scrollAreaRef.current.scrollTop = scrollAreaRef.current.scrollHeight;
    }
  }, [messages]);


  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 bg-gradient-to-r from-teal-500 to-teal-600 text-white">
        <h3 className="font-semibold">AI Task Assistant</h3>
        <Button
          variant="ghost"
          size="sm"
          onClick={onClose}
          className="text-white hover:bg-white/20"
        >
          <X className="h-4 w-4" />
        </Button>
      </div>

      {/* Messages */}
      <div className="flex-1 p-4 overflow-y-auto max-h-[300px]" ref={scrollAreaRef}>
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <AnimatePresence>
            {messages.map((message) => (
              <motion.div
                key={message.id}
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
                transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}
                className={`flex ${message.role === 'user' ? 'justify-end' : 'justify-start'}`}
              >
                <div
                  className={`max-w-[80%] rounded-lg px-4 py-2 ${
                    message.role === 'user'
                      ? 'bg-teal-500 text-white rounded-br-none'
                      : 'bg-gray-100 dark:bg-gray-700 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 rounded-bl-none'
                  }`}
                >
                  <p>{message.content}</p>
                  <p className={`text-xs mt-1 ${message.role === 'user' ? 'text-teal-100' : 'text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400'}`}>
                    {message.timestamp.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })}
                  </p>
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            ))}
          </AnimatePresence>

          {isLoading && (
            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              className="flex justify-start"
            >
              <div className="max-w-[80%] bg-gray-100 dark:bg-gray-700 text-gray-800 dark:text-gray-200 rounded-lg px-4 py-2 rounded-bl-none">
                <div className="flex space-x-2">
                  <div className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-gray-400 animate-bounce"></div>
                  <div className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-gray-400 animate-bounce delay-75"></div>
                  <div className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-gray-400 animate-bounce delay-150"></div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </motion.div>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Input Area */}
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="p-4 border-t border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 bg-white dark:bg-gray-800">
        <div className="flex space-x-2">
          <Input
            value={inputMessage}
            onChange={(e) => setInputMessage(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Ask about your tasks..."
            className="flex-1 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-gray-700 dark:text-white"
            disabled={isLoading}
          />
          <Button type="submit" disabled={isLoading || !inputMessage.trim()} className="bg-teal-500 hover:bg-teal-600">
            <Send className="h-4 w-4" />
          </Button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
}

'use client';

import * as React from 'react';
import { Moon, Sun } from 'lucide-react';
import { useTheme } from 'next-themes';

import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';

export function ModeToggle() {
  const { theme, setTheme } = useTheme();

  return (
    <Button
      variant="ghost"
      size="icon"
      onClick={() => setTheme(theme === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark')}
      aria-label="Toggle theme"
    >
      <Sun className="h-5 w-5 rotate-0 scale-100 transition-all dark:-rotate-90 dark:scale-0" />
      <Moon className="absolute h-5 w-5 rotate-90 scale-0 transition-all dark:rotate-0 dark:scale-100" />
    </Button>
  );
}

import * as React from "react"
import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const badgeVariants = cva(
  "inline-flex items-center rounded-md border px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-semibold transition-colors focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring focus:ring-offset-2",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default:
          "border-transparent bg-primary text-primary-foreground shadow-xs",
        secondary:
          "border-transparent bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80",
        destructive:
          "border-transparent bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground shadow-xs",
        outline: "text-foreground",
        success: "border-transparent bg-green-100 text-green-800 dark:bg-green-900/30 dark:text-green-300",
        warning: "border-transparent bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800 dark:bg-yellow-900/30 dark:text-yellow-300",
        danger: "border-transparent bg-red-100 text-red-800 dark:bg-red-900/30 dark:text-red-300",
        high: "border-transparent bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground shadow-xs",
        medium: "border-transparent bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80",
        low: "border border-input bg-background text-foreground",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
    },
  }
)

export interface BadgeProps
  extends React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>,
    VariantProps<typeof badgeVariants> {}

function Badge({ className, variant, ...props }: BadgeProps) {
  return (
    <div className={cn(badgeVariants({ variant, className }))} {...props} />
  )
}

export { Badge, badgeVariants }

FILE: frontend\src\components\ui\button.tsx
============================================================
import * as React from "react"
import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"
import { cva, type VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const buttonVariants = cva(
  "inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-all disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4 shrink-0 [&_svg]:shrink-0 outline-none focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive",
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default: "bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90",
        destructive:
          "bg-destructive text-white hover:bg-destructive/90 focus-visible:ring-destructive/20 dark:focus-visible:ring-destructive/40 dark:bg-destructive/60",
        outline:
          "border bg-background shadow-xs hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:bg-input/30 dark:border-input dark:hover:bg-input/50",
        secondary:
          "bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80",
        ghost:
          "hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground dark:hover:bg-accent/50",
        link: "text-primary underline-offset-4 hover:underline",
      },
      size: {
        default: "h-9 px-4 py-2 has-[>svg]:px-3",
        sm: "h-8 rounded-md gap-1.5 px-3 has-[>svg]:px-2.5",
        lg: "h-10 rounded-md px-6 has-[>svg]:px-4",
        icon: "size-9",
        "icon-sm": "size-8",
        "icon-lg": "size-10",
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: "default",
      size: "default",
    },
  }
)

function Button({
  className,
  variant = "default",
  size = "default",
  asChild = false,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<"button"> &
  VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> & {
    asChild?: boolean
  }) {
  const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button"

  return (
    <Comp
      data-slot="button"
      data-variant={variant}
      data-size={size}
      className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

export { Button, buttonVariants }

import * as React from "react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

function Card({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
  return (
    <div
      data-slot="card"
      className={cn(
        "bg-card text-card-foreground flex flex-col gap-6 rounded-xl border py-6 shadow-sm",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function CardHeader({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
  return (
    <div
      data-slot="card-header"
      className={cn(
        "@container/card-header grid auto-rows-min grid-rows-[auto_auto] items-start gap-2 px-6 has-data-[slot=card-action]:grid-cols-[1fr_auto] [.border-b]:pb-6",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function CardTitle({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
  return (
    <div
      data-slot="card-title"
      className={cn("leading-none font-semibold", className)}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function CardDescription({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
  return (
    <div
      data-slot="card-description"
      className={cn("text-muted-foreground text-sm", className)}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function CardAction({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
  return (
    <div
      data-slot="card-action"
      className={cn(
        "col-start-2 row-span-2 row-start-1 self-start justify-self-end",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function CardContent({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
  return (
    <div
      data-slot="card-content"
      className={cn("px-6", className)}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function CardFooter({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
  return (
    <div
      data-slot="card-footer"
      className={cn("flex items-center px-6 [.border-t]:pt-6", className)}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

export {
  Card,
  CardHeader,
  CardFooter,
  CardTitle,
  CardAction,
  CardDescription,
  CardContent,
}

"use client"

import * as React from "react"
import * as CheckboxPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-checkbox"
import { Check } from "lucide-react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

const Checkbox = React.forwardRef<
  React.ElementRef<typeof CheckboxPrimitive.Root>,
  React.ComponentPropsWithoutRef<typeof CheckboxPrimitive.Root>
>(({ className, ...props }, ref) => (
  <CheckboxPrimitive.Root
    ref={ref}
    className={cn(
      "peer h-4 w-4 shrink-0 rounded-sm border border-primary ring-offset-background focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring focus-visible:ring-offset-2 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 data-[state=checked]:bg-primary data-[state=checked]:text-primary-foreground",
      className
    )}
    {...props}
  >
    <CheckboxPrimitive.Indicator
      className={cn("flex items-center justify-center text-current")}
    >
      <Check className="h-4 w-4" />
    </CheckboxPrimitive.Indicator>
  </CheckboxPrimitive.Root>
))
Checkbox.displayName = CheckboxPrimitive.Root.displayName

============================================================
FILE: frontend\src\components\ui\form.tsx
============================================================
"use client"

import * as React from "react"
import type * as LabelPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-label"
import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot"
import {
  Controller,
  FormProvider,
  useFormContext,
  useFormState,
  type ControllerProps,
  type FieldPath,
  type FieldValues,
} from "react-hook-form"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"
import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label"

const Form = FormProvider

type FormFieldContextValue<
  TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
  TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>,
> = {
  name: TName
}

const FormFieldContext = React.createContext<FormFieldContextValue>(
  {} as FormFieldContextValue
)

const FormField = <
  TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
  TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>,
>({
  ...props
}: ControllerProps<TFieldValues, TName>) => {
  return (
    <FormFieldContext.Provider value={{ name: props.name }}>
      <Controller {...props} />
    </FormFieldContext.Provider>
  )
}

const useFormField = () => {
  const fieldContext = React.useContext(FormFieldContext)
  const itemContext = React.useContext(FormItemContext)
  const { getFieldState } = useFormContext()
  const formState = useFormState({ name: fieldContext.name })
  const fieldState = getFieldState(fieldContext.name, formState)

  if (!fieldContext) {
    throw new Error("useFormField should be used within <FormField>")
  }

  const { id } = itemContext

  return {
    id,
    name: fieldContext.name,
    formItemId: `${id}-form-item`,
    formDescriptionId: `${id}-form-item-description`,
    formMessageId: `${id}-form-item-message`,
    ...fieldState,
  }
}

type FormItemContextValue = {
  id: string
}

const FormItemContext = React.createContext<FormItemContextValue>(
  {} as FormItemContextValue
)

function FormItem({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
  const id = React.useId()

  return (
    <FormItemContext.Provider value={{ id }}>
      <div
        data-slot="form-item"
        className={cn("grid gap-2", className)}
        {...props}
      />
    </FormItemContext.Provider>
  )
}

function FormLabel({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<typeof LabelPrimitive.Root>) {
  const { error, formItemId } = useFormField()

  return (
    <Label
      data-slot="form-label"
      data-error={!!error}
      className={cn("data-[error=true]:text-destructive", className)}
      htmlFor={formItemId}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function FormControl({ ...props }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Slot>) {
  const { error, formItemId, formDescriptionId, formMessageId } = useFormField()

  return (
    <Slot
      data-slot="form-control"
      id={formItemId}
      aria-describedby={
        !error
          ? `${formDescriptionId}`
          : `${formDescriptionId} ${formMessageId}`
      }
      aria-invalid={!!error}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function FormDescription({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"p">) {
  const { formDescriptionId } = useFormField()

  return (
    <p
      data-slot="form-description"
      id={formDescriptionId}
      className={cn("text-muted-foreground text-sm", className)}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function FormMessage({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"p">) {
  const { error, formMessageId } = useFormField()
  const body = error ? String(error?.message ?? "") : props.children

  if (!body) {
    return null
  }

  return (
    <p
      data-slot="form-message"
      id={formMessageId}
      className={cn("text-destructive text-sm", className)}
      {...props}
    >
      {body}
    </p>
  )
}

export {
  useFormField,
  Form,
  FormItem,
  FormLabel,
  FormControl,
  FormDescription,
  FormMessage,
  FormField,
}

        "file:text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground selection:bg-primary selection:text-primary-foreground dark:bg-input/30 border-input h-9 w-full min-w-0 rounded-md border bg-transparent px-3 py-1 text-base shadow-xs transition-[color,box-shadow] outline-none file:inline-flex file:h-7 file:border-0 file:bg-transparent file:text-sm file:font-medium disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 md:text-sm",
        "focus-visible:border-teal-500 focus-visible:ring-teal-500/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px]",
        "aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive",
        className
      )}
      {...props}

"use client"

import {
  CircleCheckIcon,
  InfoIcon,
  Loader2Icon,
  OctagonXIcon,
  TriangleAlertIcon,
} from "lucide-react"
import { useTheme } from "next-themes"
import { Toaster as Sonner, type ToasterProps } from "sonner"

const Toaster = ({ ...props }: ToasterProps) => {
  const { theme = "system" } = useTheme()

  return (
    <Sonner
      theme={theme as ToasterProps["theme"]}
      className="toaster group"
      icons={{
        success: <CircleCheckIcon className="size-4" />,
        info: <InfoIcon className="size-4" />,
        warning: <TriangleAlertIcon className="size-4" />,
        error: <OctagonXIcon className="size-4" />,
        loading: <Loader2Icon className="size-4 animate-spin" />,
      }}
      style={
        {
          "--normal-bg": "var(--popover)",
          "--normal-text": "var(--popover-foreground)",
          "--normal-border": "var(--border)",
          "--border-radius": "var(--radius)",
        } as React.CSSProperties
      }
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

"use client"

import * as React from "react"

import { cn } from "@/lib/utils"

function Tabs({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<typeof TabsPrimitive.Root>) {
  return (
    <TabsPrimitive.Root
      data-slot="tabs"
      className={cn("flex flex-col gap-2", className)}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function TabsList({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<typeof TabsPrimitive.List>) {
  return (
    <TabsPrimitive.List
      data-slot="tabs-list"
      className={cn(
        "bg-muted text-muted-foreground inline-flex h-9 w-fit items-center justify-center rounded-lg p-[3px]",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

  className,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<typeof TabsPrimitive.Trigger>) {
  return (
    <TabsPrimitive.Trigger
      data-slot="tabs-trigger"
      className={cn(
        "data-[state=active]:bg-background dark:data-[state=active]:text-foreground focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:outline-ring dark:data-[state=active]:border-input dark:data-[state=active]:bg-input/30 text-foreground dark:text-muted-foreground inline-flex h-[calc(100%-1px)] flex-1 items-center justify-center gap-1.5 rounded-md border border-transparent px-2 py-1 text-sm font-medium whitespace-nowrap transition-[color,box-shadow] focus-visible:ring-[3px] focus-visible:outline-1 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 data-[state=active]:shadow-sm [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg]:shrink-0 [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4",
        className
      )}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

function TabsContent({
  className,
  ...props
}: React.ComponentProps<typeof TabsPrimitive.Content>) {

    <TabsPrimitive.Content
      data-slot="tabs-content"
      className={cn("flex-1 outline-none", className)}
      {...props}
    />
  )
}

apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: ai-agent-deployment
  namespace: default
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: ai-agent
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: ai-agent
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: ai-agent
        image: YOUR_REGISTRY/ai-agent:latest  # Replace with your container registry URL
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8000
        env:
        - name: OPENAI_API_KEY
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: ai-agent-secrets
              key: OPENAI_API_KEY
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "500m"

    targetPort: 8000
  type: ClusterIP

# Kubernetes Deployment Configuration

This directory contains Kubernetes manifests for deploying the Todo application to Oracle Container Engine for Kubernetes (OKE).

## Overview

The application consists of multiple microservices:
- **Backend**: FastAPI server handling business logic and database operations
- **Frontend**: Next.js/React application serving the user interface
- **AI Agent**: AI-powered assistant component
- **MCP Server**: Model Context Protocol server

## Prerequisites

Before deploying to Oracle Cloud Infrastructure (OCI):

1. **OCI Account**: Ensure you have access to an OCI account
2. **OKE Cluster**: Have an OKE cluster running
3. **OCI CLI**: Install and configure the OCI CLI
4. **kubectl**: Install kubectl and connect to your OKE cluster
5. **Container Registry**: Set up Oracle Cloud Container Registry (OCIR)

## Setup Steps

### 1. Configure Container Images

Update the image references in the deployment files to point to your OCIR repository:

```bash
# Replace YOUR_REGISTRY with your actual OCIR region and namespace
# Example: phx.ocir.io/tenancy_namespace/repository_name
```

### 2. Build and Push Images

Build Docker images for each service and push to OCIR:

```bash
# Build backend image
docker build -t YOUR_REGISTRY/todo-backend:latest ./backend
docker push YOUR_REGISTRY/todo-backend:latest

# Build frontend image
docker build -t YOUR_REGISTRY/todo-frontend:latest ./frontend
docker push YOUR_REGISTRY/todo-frontend:latest

# Build ai_agent image
docker build -t YOUR_REGISTRY/ai-agent:latest ./ai_agent
docker push YOUR_REGISTRY/ai-agent:latest

# Build mcp-server image
docker build -t YOUR_REGISTRY/mcp-server:latest ./mcp-server
docker push YOUR_REGISTRY/mcp-server:latest
```

### 3. Update Secrets

Encode your sensitive information in base64 format and update the secrets.yaml file:

```bash
# Encode database URL
echo -n 'your_database_url_here' | base64

# Encode OpenAI API key
echo -n 'your_openai_api_key_here' | base64
```

### 4. Deploy to OKE

Apply the Kubernetes manifests:

```bash
# Apply all configurations
kubectl apply -f production-deployment.yaml

# Or apply individual files
kubectl apply -f secrets.yaml
kubectl apply -f backend-deployment.yaml
kubectl apply -f backend-service.yaml
kubectl apply -f frontend-deployment.yaml
kubectl apply -f frontend-service.yaml
kubectl apply -f ai-agent-deployment.yaml
kubectl apply -f ai-agent-service.yaml
kubectl apply -f mcp-server-deployment.yaml
kubectl apply -f mcp-server-service.yaml
```

### 5. Verify Deployment

Check the status of your deployments:

```bash
kubectl get pods
kubectl get services
kubectl get deployments
```

## Environment Variables

The application expects the following environment variables to be configured via Kubernetes secrets:

- `DATABASE_URL`: Connection string for the PostgreSQL database
- `OPENAI_API_KEY`: API key for OpenAI integration (if using AI features)

## Scaling

To scale deployments:

```bash
# Scale backend to 3 replicas
kubectl scale deployment backend-deployment --replicas=3

# Scale frontend to 2 replicas
kubectl scale deployment frontend-deployment --replicas=2
```

## Troubleshooting

1. Check pod logs:
   ```bash
   kubectl logs -f deployment/backend-deployment
   kubectl logs -f deployment/frontend-deployment
   ```

2. Check service endpoints:
   ```bash
   kubectl get svc frontend-service  # Note the external IP if using LoadBalancer
   ```

3. Describe resources for detailed information:
   ```bash
   kubectl describe deployment backend-deployment
   kubectl describe pod POD_NAME
   ```

FILE: mcp-server\main.py
============================================================
# mcp-server\main.py
from mcp.server.fastmcp import FastMCP
import httpx
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any

# Initialize FastMCP server
mcp = FastMCP("TodoManager")

BACKEND_URL = "http://localhost:8000"  # Changed from /api/v1 to root since our API endpoints are at /api/{user_id}/...

@mcp.tool()
async def get_tasks(session_token: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """
    Retrieve all tasks for the authenticated user.
    :param session_token: The session token of the user.
    """
    try:
        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:  # Added timeout for better error handling
            response = await client.get(
                f"{BACKEND_URL}/tasks/",
                headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {session_token}"}
            )
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
    except httpx.TimeoutException:
        raise Exception("Database connection timeout")
    except httpx.HTTPStatusError as e:
        if e.response.status_code == 401:
            raise Exception("Session expired or invalid")
        elif e.response.status_code == 404:
            raise Exception("Tasks not found")
        else:
            raise Exception(f"HTTP error {e.response.status_code}: {e.response.text}")
    except httpx.RequestError as e:
        raise Exception(f"Request error: {str(e)}")

@mcp.tool()
async def create_task(session_token: str, title: str, description: Optional[str] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Create a new todo item.
    :param session_token: The session token of the user.
    :param title: The title of the task.
    :param description: Optional description of the task.
    """
    try:
        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:  # Added timeout for better error handling
            payload = {"title": title}
            if description:
                payload["description"] = description

            response = await client.post(
                f"{BACKEND_URL}/tasks/",
                json=payload,
                headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {session_token}"}
            )
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
    except httpx.TimeoutException:
        raise Exception("Database connection timeout")
    except httpx.HTTPStatusError as e:
        if e.response.status_code == 401:
            raise Exception("Session expired or invalid")
        else:
            raise Exception(f"HTTP error {e.response.status_code}: {e.response.text}")
    except httpx.RequestError as e:
        raise Exception(f"Request error: {str(e)}")

@mcp.tool()
async def update_task(
    session_token: str,
    task_id: str,  # Changed from int to str to match our UUID task IDs
    title: Optional[str] = None,
    status: Optional[str] = None,
    description: Optional[str] = None
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Update an existing task.
    :param session_token: The session token of the user.
    :param task_id: The ID of the task to update.
    :param title: New title for the task.
    :param status: New status (e.g., 'pending', 'completed').
    :param description: New description for the task.
    """
    try:
        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:  # Added timeout for better error handling
            payload = {}
            if title is not None:
                payload["title"] = title
            if status is not None:
                payload["status"] = status
            if description is not None:
                payload["description"] = description

            response = await client.put(
                f"{BACKEND_URL}/tasks/{task_id}",
                json=payload,
                headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {session_token}"}
            )
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
    except httpx.TimeoutException:
        raise Exception("Database connection timeout")
    except httpx.HTTPStatusError as e:
        if e.response.status_code == 401:
            raise Exception("Session expired or invalid")
        elif e.response.status_code == 404:
            raise Exception("Task not found")
        else:
            raise Exception(f"HTTP error {e.response.status_code}: {e.response.text}")
    except httpx.RequestError as e:
        raise Exception(f"Request error: {str(e)}")

@mcp.tool()
async def delete_task(session_token: str, task_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:  # Changed from int to str to match our UUID task IDs
    """
    Delete a task.
    :param session_token: The session token of the user.
    :param task_id: The ID of the task to delete.
    """
    try:
        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=30.0) as client:  # Added timeout for better error handling
            response = await client.delete(
                f"{BACKEND_URL}/tasks/{task_id}",
                headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {session_token}"}
            )
            response.raise_for_status()
            return response.json()
    except httpx.TimeoutException:
        raise Exception("Database connection timeout")
    except httpx.HTTPStatusError as e:
        if e.response.status_code == 401:
            raise Exception("Session expired or invalid")
        elif e.response.status_code == 404:
            raise Exception("Task not found")
        else:
            raise Exception(f"HTTP error {e.response.status_code}: {e.response.text}")
    except httpx.RequestError as e:
        raise Exception(f"Request error: {str(e)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    mcp.run()

# Implementation Plan: Phase II - Full-Stack Web Application

**Feature**: Phase II - Full-Stack Web Application
**Spec File**: [001-phase-ii-full-stack-web-app.spec.md](001-phase-ii-full-stack-web-app.spec.md)
**Created**: 2025-12-28
**Status**: Draft

## Technical Context

- **Backend**: FastAPI with Python 3.10+
- **Database**: Neon PostgreSQL with SQLModel
- **Authentication**: Better Auth with JWT
- **Frontend**: Next.js 14+ with App Router
- **Styling**: Tailwind CSS
- **Monorepo**: pnpm or npm workspaces
- **API Pattern**: RESTful with `/api/{user_id}/tasks` endpoints

## Architecture Overview

The application will follow a monorepo structure with separate frontend and backend directories. The backend will provide a RESTful API that the frontend consumes. Authentication will be handled by Better Auth with JWT tokens for session management.

## Phase 0: Research & Setup

### Research Tasks
- **R01**: Research Best practices for FastAPI + SQLModel + Neon PostgreSQL integration
- **R02**: Research Best practices for Better Auth + JWT implementation in FastAPI
- **R03**: Research Best practices for Next.js 14 + App Router + Tailwind CSS
- **R04**: Research Best practices for monorepo setup with pnpm/npm workspaces

### Setup Tasks
- **S01**: Create monorepo structure with frontend/ and backend/ directories
- **S02**: Set up shared configuration files at root level
- **S03**: Configure pnpm or npm workspaces for monorepo management
- **S04**: Set up development, staging, and production environments

## Phase 1: Data Model & API Contracts

### Data Model Implementation
- **DM01**: Implement User model with SQLModel (UUID, email, username, password_hash, timestamps)
- **DM02**: Implement Task model with SQLModel (UUID, user_id FK, title, description, status, priority, due_date, timestamps)
- **DM03**: Implement Session model with SQLModel (UUID, user_id FK, jwt_token, expiration, timestamps)
- **DM04**: Set up database connection and migration system for Neon PostgreSQL

### API Contract Implementation
- **AC01**: Implement GET `/api/{user_id}/tasks` endpoint with authentication validation
- **AC02**: Implement POST `/api/{user_id}/tasks` endpoint with request validation
- **AC03**: Implement PUT `/api/{user_id}/tasks/{task_id}` endpoint with request validation
- **AC04**: Implement DELETE `/api/{user_id}/tasks/{task_id}` endpoint with proper response codes
- **AC05**: Implement proper error handling and status codes across all endpoints
- **AC06**: Implement request validation and sanitization middleware
- **AC07**: Implement rate limiting for API endpoints
- **AC08**: Implement CORS configuration for frontend access

## Phase 2: Authentication System

### Better Auth Integration
- **AA01**: Set up Better Auth for user registration and login
- **AA02**: Configure JWT token generation and validation
- **AA03**: Implement email verification for new user accounts
- **AA04**: Implement password reset functionality
- **AA05**: Implement secure session management with token refresh
- **AA06**: Implement proper logout functionality that invalidates tokens
- **AA07**: Implement rate limiting for authentication endpoints

### Authorization Implementation
- **AU01**: Implement middleware to validate JWT tokens on protected endpoints
- **AU02**: Implement user_id validation to ensure users can only access their own tasks
- **AU03**: Implement proper error responses for unauthorized access attempts

## Phase 3: Frontend Implementation

### Core UI Components
- **FC01**: Create responsive layout with Tailwind CSS
- **FC02**: Implement task list component to display user's tasks
- **FC03**: Implement task creation form with validation
- **FC04**: Implement task editing form with validation
- **FC05**: Implement task completion toggle with visual feedback
- **FC06**: Implement task deletion with confirmation
- **FC07**: Implement pagination for task lists

### Authentication UI
- **FA01**: Create login page with Better Auth integration
- **FA02**: Create registration page with Better Auth integration
- **FA03**: Implement protected routes that require authentication
- **FA04**: Implement logout functionality
- **FA05**: Implement password reset UI

### API Integration
- **FI01**: Create API client to interact with backend endpoints
- **FI02**: Implement data fetching and caching for task operations
- **FI03**: Implement error handling for API responses
- **FI04**: Implement loading states and user feedback

## Phase 4: Integration & Testing

### Integration Tasks
- **IT01**: Connect frontend to backend API endpoints
- **IT02**: Test authentication flow from registration to task operations
- **IT03**: Verify user isolation (users can only access their own tasks)
- **IT04**: Test all CRUD operations for tasks
- **IT05**: Test task completion functionality
- **IT06**: Verify responsive design across different devices

### Testing Tasks
- **TE01**: Write unit tests for backend API endpoints
- **TE02**: Write integration tests for authentication flow
- **TE03**: Write unit tests for frontend components
- **TE04**: Write end-to-end tests for critical user journeys
- **TE05**: Performance testing to ensure API response times under 500ms

## Phase 5: Deployment & Optimization

### Deployment Setup
- **DS01**: Set up Neon PostgreSQL database for production
- **DS02**: Configure environment variables for different environments
- **DS03**: Set up CI/CD pipeline for automated testing and deployment
- **DS04**: Deploy backend API to hosting platform
- **DS05**: Deploy frontend application to hosting platform

### Optimization Tasks
- **OP01**: Optimize database queries for performance
- **OP02**: Implement caching strategies where appropriate
- **OP03**: Optimize frontend bundle size and loading times
- **OP04**: Set up monitoring and logging for production
- **OP05**: Performance testing under load conditions

## Risk Analysis

### High-Risk Areas
- **RISK-01**: Authentication security - Ensure JWT tokens are properly secured and validated
- **RISK-02**: Data isolation - Critical that users can only access their own data
- **RISK-03**: API performance - Ensure endpoints meet 500ms response time requirement

### Mitigation Strategies
- **MIT-01**: Implement comprehensive authentication testing and security audits
- **MIT-02**: Implement strict user_id validation in all API endpoints
- **MIT-03**: Set up performance monitoring and implement caching where needed

## Success Criteria Verification

Each success criterion from the spec will be verified:
- **SC-001**: Users can register, log in, and access task management system
- **SC-002**: All API endpoints respond within 500ms for 95% of requests
- **SC-003**: Users can perform all basic task operations through web interface
- **SC-004**: Authentication system prevents unauthorized access with 100% accuracy
- **SC-005**: Web interface is responsive across devices
- **SC-006**: System supports 100 concurrent users without degradation
- **SC-007**: 95% of users can complete registration/login without assistance

# Feature Specification: Phase II - Full-Stack Web Application

**Feature Branch**: `001-phase-ii-full-stack-web-app`
**Created**: 2025-12-28
**Status**: Draft
**Input**: User description: "Transition from Phase I (Console Application) to Phase II (Full-Stack Web Application) with Neon PostgreSQL, Better Auth, and monorepo structure"

## User Scenarios & Testing *(mandatory)*

### User Story 1 - Web-based Task Management (Priority: P1)

As a user, I want to access my task management system through a web interface so that I can manage my tasks from any device with a browser.

**Why this priority**: This is the core functionality that differentiates Phase II from Phase I - providing a web interface instead of a console application.

**Independent Test**: Can be fully tested by accessing the web application, logging in, and performing basic task operations (add, list, update, delete, complete). Delivers the core value of web-based task management.

**Acceptance Scenarios**:

1. **Given** I am a registered user with valid credentials, **When** I access the web application and log in, **Then** I can view my task dashboard
2. **Given** I am logged into the web application, **When** I create a new task, **Then** the task appears in my task list
3. **Given** I have tasks in my list, **When** I mark a task as complete, **Then** the task status updates to completed

---

### User Story 2 - User Authentication & Authorization (Priority: P1)

As a user, I want to securely log in to the web application so that my tasks are protected and only accessible to me.

**Why this priority**: Security is fundamental to the application. Without proper authentication, the task management system cannot be safely deployed.

**Independent Test**: Can be fully tested by registering a new user, logging in, and verifying that only that user's tasks are accessible. Delivers the core security value.

**Acceptance Scenarios**:

1. **Given** I am a new user, **When** I register with valid credentials, **Then** I can log in with those credentials
2. **Given** I am logged in, **When** I access the task API, **Then** I can only access my own tasks
3. **Given** I am logged in, **When** my session expires, **Then** I am redirected to the login page

---

### User Story 3 - Task CRUD Operations via Web API (Priority: P2)

As a user, I want to perform all basic task operations (Create, Read, Update, Delete) through the web interface so that I have full control over my tasks.

**Why this priority**: This provides the complete task management functionality that users expect from the system.

**Independent Test**: Can be fully tested by performing all CRUD operations through the web interface. Delivers complete task management capabilities.

**Acceptance Scenarios**:

1. **Given** I am logged in, **When** I submit a POST request to `/api/{user_id}/tasks`, **Then** a new task is created
2. **Given** I have tasks, **When** I submit a GET request to `/api/{user_id}/tasks`, **Then** I receive my task list
3. **Given** I have a task, **When** I submit a PUT request to `/api/{user_id}/tasks/{task_id}`, **Then** the task is updated
4. **Given** I have a task, **When** I submit a DELETE request to `/api/{user_id}/tasks/{task_id}`, **Then** the task is removed

---

### User Story 4 - Task Completion Tracking (Priority: P2)

As a user, I want to mark tasks as completed so that I can track my progress and focus on remaining tasks.

**Why this priority**: This is a core feature of task management that users expect, allowing them to track completion status.

**Independent Test**: Can be fully tested by marking tasks as complete and verifying the status change persists. Delivers task completion tracking functionality.

**Acceptance Scenarios**:

1. **Given** I have an incomplete task, **When** I mark it as complete, **Then** its status changes to completed
2. **Given** I have completed tasks, **When** I view my task list, **Then** I can distinguish completed from incomplete tasks

---

### User Story 5 - Responsive Web Interface (Priority: P3)

As a user, I want to access the task management system on different devices so that I can manage my tasks anywhere.

**Why this priority**: Enhances user experience by providing accessibility across different devices and screen sizes.

**Independent Test**: Can be fully tested by accessing the web application on different screen sizes and verifying responsive layout. Delivers cross-device accessibility.

**Acceptance Scenarios**:

1. **Given** I am using a mobile device, **When** I access the web application, **Then** the interface adapts to the smaller screen
2. **Given** I am using a tablet, **When** I access the web application, **Then** the interface provides optimal layout for the screen size

---

### Edge Cases

- What happens when a user tries to access another user's tasks?
- How does the system handle concurrent updates to the same task?
- What happens when the database is temporarily unavailable?
- How does the system handle malformed API requests?
- What happens when a user's JWT token is invalid or expired?

## Requirements *(mandatory)*

### Functional Requirements

- **FR-001**: System MUST provide a web-based interface for task management accessible via browser
- **FR-002**: System MUST authenticate users using Better Auth with JWT tokens
- **FR-003**: System MUST store user data in Neon PostgreSQL database
- **FR-004**: System MUST implement RESTful API endpoints at `/api/{user_id}/tasks` for task operations
- **FR-005**: System MUST support GET/POST/PUT/DELETE operations on tasks
- **FR-006**: System MUST allow users to mark tasks as completed
- **FR-007**: System MUST ensure users can only access their own tasks
- **FR-008**: System MUST provide responsive web interface compatible with desktop and mobile devices
- **FR-009**: System MUST validate all API requests and return appropriate error responses
- **FR-010**: System MUST implement proper session management with JWT token refresh

### Authentication Flow Requirements

- **AF-001**: System MUST use Better Auth for user registration, login, and session management
- **AF-002**: System MUST generate JWT tokens upon successful authentication
- **AF-003**: System MUST validate JWT tokens on all protected API endpoints
- **AF-004**: System MUST implement token refresh mechanism before expiration
- **AF-005**: System MUST securely store and handle JWT tokens in browser (HttpOnly cookies or secure local storage)
- **AF-006**: System MUST implement proper logout functionality that invalidates tokens
- **AF-007**: System MUST implement password reset functionality through Better Auth
- **AF-008**: System MUST implement email verification for new user accounts
- **AF-009**: System MUST implement rate limiting for authentication endpoints to prevent brute force attacks
- **AF-010**: System MUST implement secure password hashing (handled by Better Auth)

### Monorepo Structure Requirements

- **MS-001**: System MUST organize code in a monorepo with separate frontend/ and backend/ directories
- **MS-002**: System MUST use pnpm or npm workspaces for package management across the monorepo
- **MS-003**: Backend directory MUST contain all server-side code, API endpoints, and database models
- **MS-004**: Frontend directory MUST contain all client-side code, components, and UI elements
- **MS-005**: System MUST have shared configuration files at the root level
- **MS-006**: System MUST have shared types or contracts between frontend and backend when needed
- **MS-007**: System MUST support independent development and testing of frontend and backend
- **MS-008**: System MUST have clear build and deployment scripts for both frontend and backend

### API Endpoint Requirements

- **API-001**: System MUST implement GET `/api/{user_id}/tasks` endpoint to retrieve user's tasks
  - Request: GET `/api/{user_id}/tasks` with valid JWT token in Authorization header
  - Response: 200 OK with array of task objects in JSON format
  - Response Body: `[{task_id, title, description, status, priority, due_date, created_at, updated_at, completed_at}, ...]`
  - Error Responses: 401 Unauthorized, 403 Forbidden, 404 Not Found, 500 Internal Server Error

- **API-002**: System MUST implement POST `/api/{user_id}/tasks` endpoint to create new tasks
  - Request: POST `/api/{user_id}/tasks` with valid JWT token in Authorization header
  - Request Body: `{title: string, description?: string, priority?: 'low'|'medium'|'high', due_date?: string}`
  - Response: 201 Created with created task object in JSON format
  - Response Body: `{task_id, title, description, status, priority, due_date, created_at, updated_at}`
  - Error Responses: 400 Bad Request, 401 Unauthorized, 403 Forbidden, 500 Internal Server Error

- **API-003**: System MUST implement PUT `/api/{user_id}/tasks/{task_id}` endpoint to update tasks
  - Request: PUT `/api/{user_id}/tasks/{task_id}` with valid JWT token in Authorization header
  - Request Body: `{title?: string, description?: string, status?: 'pending'|'completed', priority?: 'low'|'medium'|'high', due_date?: string}`
  - Response: 200 OK with updated task object in JSON format
  - Response Body: `{task_id, title, description, status, priority, due_date, created_at, updated_at, completed_at}`
  - Error Responses: 400 Bad Request, 401 Unauthorized, 403 Forbidden, 404 Not Found, 500 Internal Server Error

- **API-004**: System MUST implement DELETE `/api/{user_id}/tasks/{task_id}` endpoint to delete tasks
  - Request: DELETE `/api/{user_id}/tasks/{task_id}` with valid JWT token in Authorization header
  - Response: 204 No Content on successful deletion
  - Error Responses: 401 Unauthorized, 403 Forbidden, 404 Not Found, 500 Internal Server Error

- **API-005**: System MUST validate that user_id in URL matches authenticated user's ID for all endpoints
- **API-006**: System MUST return appropriate HTTP status codes for all responses
- **API-007**: System MUST implement proper request validation and sanitization
- **API-008**: System MUST implement rate limiting for API endpoints to prevent abuse
- **API-009**: System MUST include proper CORS headers to allow frontend access
- **API-010**: System MUST implement pagination for GET `/api/{user_id}/tasks` when user has many tasks

### Key Entities

- **User**: Represents a registered user with authentication credentials, unique identifier, and profile information
  - user_id: UUID (Primary Key)
  - email: String (Unique, Required)
  - username: String (Unique, Optional)
  - password_hash: String (Required, from Better Auth)
  - created_at: DateTime (Required, Auto-generated)
  - updated_at: DateTime (Required, Auto-generated)
  - is_active: Boolean (Default: true)

- **Task**: Represents a user's task with title, description, status (pending/completed), creation date, and user relationship
  - task_id: UUID (Primary Key)
  - user_id: UUID (Foreign Key to User, Required)
  - title: String (Required, Max 255 chars)
  - description: Text (Optional)
  - status: String (Enum: 'pending', 'completed', Default: 'pending')
  - priority: String (Enum: 'low', 'medium', 'high', Default: 'medium')
  - due_date: DateTime (Optional)
  - created_at: DateTime (Required, Auto-generated)
  - updated_at: DateTime (Required, Auto-generated)
  - completed_at: DateTime (Optional, set when status becomes 'completed')

- **Session**: Represents an authenticated user session with JWT token, expiration, and user association
  - session_id: UUID (Primary Key)
  - user_id: UUID (Foreign Key to User, Required)
  - jwt_token: String (Required, Indexed)
  - expires_at: DateTime (Required)
  - created_at: DateTime (Required, Auto-generated)
  - is_active: Boolean (Default: true)

## Success Criteria *(mandatory)*

### Measurable Outcomes

- **SC-001**: Users can successfully register, log in, and access the task management system through the web interface
- **SC-002**: All API endpoints respond within 500ms for 95% of requests under normal load
- **SC-003**: Users can perform all basic task operations (Add, Delete, Update, List, Complete) through the web interface
- **SC-004**: Authentication system prevents unauthorized access to user data with 100% accuracy
- **SC-005**: Web interface is responsive and functional across desktop, tablet, and mobile devices
- **SC-006**: System supports at least 100 concurrent users without performance degradation
- **SC-007**: 95% of users can complete the registration and login process without assistance

FILE: specs\mcp-tools.md

# Model Context Protocol (MCP) Tools Specification

## Overview
This specification defines the Model Context Protocol (MCP) server structure for the TaskFlow application. The MCP server exposes tools for task management operations that can be used by AI agents and other services.

## Architecture
The MCP server follows a stateless, RESTful architecture pattern that integrates with the existing TaskFlow backend services. It provides a standardized interface for external systems to interact with task management functionality.

## Required Tools

### 1. add_task
- **Purpose**: Create a new task for a specific user
- **Parameters**:
  - `user_id` (string, required): Unique identifier of the user
  - `title` (string, required): Title of the task
  - `description` (string, optional): Detailed description of the task
  - `priority` (string, optional): Priority level (low, medium, high), defaults to "medium"
  - `due_date` (string, optional): Due date in ISO 8601 format
- **Response**: Task object with all fields including the generated task ID
- **Authentication**: Requires valid user context
- **Authorization**: User must have permission to create tasks for the specified user_id

### 2. list_tasks
- **Purpose**: Retrieve all tasks for a specific user
- **Parameters**:
  - `user_id` (string, required): Unique identifier of the user
  - `status` (string, optional): Filter by status (pending, completed)
  - `priority` (string, optional): Filter by priority (low, medium, high)
- **Response**: Array of task objects matching the criteria
- **Authentication**: Requires valid user context
- **Authorization**: User must have permission to view tasks for the specified user_id

### 3. update_task
- **Purpose**: Update properties of an existing task
- **Parameters**:
  - `user_id` (string, required): Unique identifier of the user
  - `task_id` (string, required): Unique identifier of the task to update
  - `title` (string, optional): New title of the task
  - `description` (string, optional): New description of the task
  - `status` (string, optional): New status (pending, completed)
  - `priority` (string, optional): New priority level (low, medium, high)
  - `due_date` (string, optional): New due date in ISO 8601 format
- **Response**: Updated task object
- **Authentication**: Requires valid user context
- **Authorization**: User must have permission to update tasks for the specified user_id

### 4. delete_task
- **Purpose**: Remove a specific task
- **Parameters**:
  - `user_id` (string, required): Unique identifier of the user
  - `task_id` (string, required): Unique identifier of the task to delete
- **Response**: Empty response with success status
- **Authentication**: Requires valid user context
- **Authorization**: User must have permission to delete tasks for the specified user_id

### 5. complete_task
- **Purpose**: Mark a specific task as completed
- **Parameters**:
  - `user_id` (string, required): Unique identifier of the user
  - `task_id` (string, required): Unique identifier of the task to complete
- **Response**: Updated task object with status "completed" and completed_at timestamp
- **Authentication**: Requires valid user context
- **Authorization**: User must have permission to update tasks for the specified user_id

## Implementation Requirements

### Authentication & Authorization
- Each tool must validate the `user_id` parameter against the authenticated user's permissions
- For admin users, access to any user's tasks is permitted
- For regular users, access is restricted to their own tasks only
- All operations must verify that the requesting user has appropriate permissions

### Error Handling
- Return appropriate HTTP status codes for different error conditions
- Provide meaningful error messages that help diagnose issues
- Ensure consistent error response format across all tools

### Data Validation
- Validate all input parameters according to the existing model constraints
- Ensure data integrity by checking foreign key relationships
- Apply the same validation rules as the existing TaskFlow API

### Database Integration
- Use the existing database connection and ORM patterns
- Follow the same transaction management practices as the main API
- Maintain consistency with existing data models and relationships

## Security Considerations
- All tools must implement proper input sanitization
- Prevent SQL injection and other common vulnerabilities
- Ensure proper access control to prevent unauthorized task manipulation
- Log all operations for audit purposes

## Performance Requirements
- Tools should respond within 500ms for typical operations
- Implement proper indexing for efficient queries
- Use connection pooling for database operations
- Cache frequently accessed data where appropriate

## Testing Requirements
- Each tool must have comprehensive unit tests
- Integration tests must verify proper database interactions
- Security tests must validate proper access controls
- Performance tests must verify response time requirements

FILE: specs\features\chatbot.md
============================================================
# Stateless Chat Architecture Specification

## Overview
This specification defines a stateless chat architecture for the TaskFlow application. The architecture uses the OpenAI Agents SDK to process natural language queries, interacts with MCP tools for task management, and persists conversation history in the Neon PostgreSQL database.

## Architecture Pattern
The chat system follows a stateless, event-driven architecture where each request contains all necessary context for processing. No server-side session state is maintained between requests, ensuring scalability and reliability.

## API Endpoint

### POST /api/{user_id}/chat
- **Purpose**: Process natural language input and generate appropriate responses
- **Path Parameters**:
  - `user_id` (string, required): Unique identifier of the user making the request
- **Request Body**:
  - `message` (string, required): Natural language message from the user
  - `context` (object, optional): Additional context for the conversation
    - `conversation_id` (string, optional): Identifier for the conversation thread
    - `timestamp` (string, optional): ISO 8601 timestamp of the message
- **Response**:
  - `response` (string): Natural language response to the user
  - `conversation_id` (string): Identifier for the conversation thread
  - `timestamp` (string): ISO 8601 timestamp of the response
  - `actions` (array, optional): List of actions taken as a result of the message
- **Authentication**: Requires valid JWT token in Authorization header
- **Authorization**: User must have permission to access their own chat endpoint

## Implementation Components

### 1. OpenAI Agents SDK Integration
- Use OpenAI's Agent framework to process natural language input
- Configure the agent with appropriate system instructions for task management
- Implement function calling to interact with MCP tools
- Handle agent responses and convert to user-friendly format

### 2. MCP Tool Integration
- Map natural language commands to appropriate MCP tools
- Implement proper error handling when MCP tools fail
- Validate user permissions before executing MCP operations
- Transform tool responses to natural language output

### 3. Conversation History Persistence
- Store conversation history in Neon PostgreSQL database
- Create a `Conversation` table with fields:
  - `id` (UUID, primary key): Unique identifier for the conversation
  - `user_id` (string, indexed): Foreign key to the user
  - `title` (string): Auto-generated title for the conversation
  - `created_at` (timestamp): When the conversation was created
  - `updated_at` (timestamp): When the conversation was last updated
- Create a `Message` table with fields:
  - `id` (UUID, primary key): Unique identifier for the message
  - `conversation_id` (UUID, indexed): Foreign key to the conversation
  - `user_id` (string): ID of the user who sent the message
  - `role` (string): Either "user" or "assistant"
  - `content` (text): The message content
  - `timestamp` (timestamp): When the message was sent
  - `metadata` (JSON): Additional metadata about the message

### 4. Natural Language Processing Flow
1. Receive user message via POST request
2. Authenticate and authorize the user
3. Create or retrieve conversation record
4. Pass message to OpenAI Agent with conversation context
5. Agent processes message and may call MCP tools
6. Store user message in database
7. Generate natural language response
8. Store assistant response in database
9. Return response to user

## Security Considerations
- Validate that the `user_id` in the path matches the authenticated user
- Implement rate limiting to prevent abuse
- Sanitize all user inputs to prevent injection attacks
- Encrypt sensitive conversation data at rest
- Implement proper access controls to prevent unauthorized access

## Error Handling
- Return appropriate HTTP status codes for different error conditions
- Provide meaningful error messages without exposing internal details
- Log errors for debugging while protecting user privacy
- Implement retry logic for transient failures

## Performance Requirements
- API responses should be delivered within 2 seconds for typical requests
- Support up to 1000 concurrent users
- Implement caching for frequently accessed data
- Optimize database queries with proper indexing

## Data Privacy
- Implement data retention policies for conversation history
- Allow users to delete their conversation history
- Comply with applicable data protection regulations
- Provide users with access to their conversation data

## Testing Requirements
- Unit tests for natural language processing components
- Integration tests for MCP tool interactions
- End-to-end tests for the complete chat flow
- Performance tests to verify response time requirements
- Security tests to validate access controls

## Conversation Management
- Automatically create new conversation when no conversation_id is provided
- Maintain conversation context for follow-up questions
- Implement conversation summarization for long-running conversations
- Allow users to list and select from previous conversations

## MCP Tool Mapping Examples
- "Add a task to buy groceries" ‚Üí `add_task` tool
- "Show me my tasks" ‚Üí `list_tasks` tool
- "Mark task 'buy groceries' as completed" ‚Üí `complete_task` tool
- "Update the due date for 'project report'" ‚Üí `update_task` tool
- "Delete the task about meeting" ‚Üí `delete_task` tool
